name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:1 King Classic
info:Stayed in June 2024
info:Other
info:11 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted June 3, 2024
msg:First of all, the configuration and appearance are standard InterContinental City Hotel. The overall decoration is good. Although it is a bit old, I still like the small storage room at the entrance. I won't see the luggage in a mess in the room. It's especially good. The bed in the king-size room is very large. It is about 2.2 meters long and can accommodate two adults and two children for a parent-child trip. The swimming pool is small but the water quality is good. Because it is outsourced, I occasionally encounter many children taking swimming lessons. The room area is very pleasant. It is an upgraded viewing room. The view of the golf course opposite and the night view of the TV tower are very nice. The room is equipped with a capsule coffee machine. A cup of black coffee in the morning is great. Special thanks to the housekeeper Zhang Yu for his meticulous and thoughtful service. The welcome fruit (quality and weight are very good) at the door, and the things I need (pure water, disposable items, etc.) are also delivered quickly. If there is a problem with the air conditioner, he will arrange a room change in time and help me move my luggage directly when I can't go back to the hotel. It is very considerate. The delayed check-out service can also be met. The overall experience is very good. The front desk is generally satisfactory, and there is no enthusiasm from the housekeeper. If I go next time, I will choose R&F InterContinental.
The location is very good. Next door is Wanda Pedestrian Street, which connects to the Locomotive Pedestrian Street. It is no problem to go shopping until 11 o'clock in the evening. It is very convenient to eat, drink and shop. It is also very convenient to take a taxi anywhere, not far away. There are also shared electric cars for walking. If you like to go to the park, Century Park is opposite. Next door is the Huoshe Hotpot opened by Deng Lun. If you like it, you can go there to check in. The decoration is good, but the taste is suitable for friends who can't eat spicy food but want to eat spicy hotpot.
Let me talk about a few small suggestions: 1. The base of the desk chair bed is worn out. It has been reported and the reply is being replaced in batches. 2. The TV has automatically shut down and restarted many times, and the remote control board often does not respond to the buttons. It is recommended to check or replace the battery regularly. There are fewer TV stations.
3. It is recommended to put the tissue on the desk, and it is also recommended to put a tissue on the bathroom sink.
4. The quality of disposable slippers is relatively poor, the bottom is thin, and the anti-slip is average.
5. No plastic slippers are prepared for swimming.
6. It is recommended to put a reminder label on the outside of the hair dryer socket. I didn't find it. I took it out to blow dry and put it back. I found a small socket in the small partition. As an old fan of InterContinental, I hope it gets better and better.
